# Text Elements
Example 1.9
    a hot-air balloon with an inflated diameter of 30ft is carrying a weight
of 800lb, which includes the weight of the hot air inside the balloon, calculate
(1) upward acceleration at sea level the instant the restraining ropes are released
(2) the maximum altitude it can achieve

assume the variation of the density in the standard atmosphere is given by  ^IcGQwGSw

where h is the altitude (in feet) and  ^tx7IGXsd

is the density (slug/ft^3) ^nsfO3eNg

solution:  ^WEcdQ6va


# Embedded files
dfaf8a57011c19c7ff572d768f0ab99479f302d4: $$\rho = 0.002377(1 - 7\times 10^{-6} h)^{4.21}$$
2d51e0c96bcceac5dd872bf587f46c3058fed262: $$\rho$$
